highlight ruby%}
require "gem"

string = "base16"
symbol = :base16
fixnum = 0
float  = 0.00
array  = Array.new
array  = ['chris', 85]
hash   = {"test" => "test"}
regexp = /[abc]/

# This is a comment
class Person
  
  attr_accessor :name
  
  def initialize(attributes = {})
    @name = attributes[:name]
  end
  
  def self.greet
    "hello"
  end
end

person1 = Person.new(:name => "Chris")
print Person::greet, " ", person1.name, "\n"
puts "another #{Person::greet} #{person1.name}"

require "gem"

string = "base16"
symbol = :base16
fixnum = 0
float  = 0.00
array  = Array.new
array  = ['chris', 85]
hash   = {"test" => "test"}
regexp = /[abc]/

# This is a comment
class Person
  
  attr_accessor :name
  
  def initialize(attributes = {})
    @name = attributes[:name]
  end
  
  def self.greet
    "hello"
  end
end

person1 = Person.new(:name => "Chris")
print Person::greet, " ", person1.name, "\n"
puts "another #{Person::greet} #{person1.name}"

symbol = :base16
fixnum = 0

    "hello"
  end

  attr_accessor :name

    @name = attributes[:name]
  end

    "hello"
  end

require "gem"

string = "base16"
symbol = :base16
fixnum = 0
float  = 0.00
array  = Array.new
array  = ['chris', 85]
hash   = {"test" => "test"}
regexp = /[abc]/

# This is a comment
class Person
  
  attr_accessor :name
  
  def initialize(attributes = {})
    @name = attributes[:name]
  end
  
  def self.greet
    "hello"
  end
end

person1 = Person.new(:name => "Chris")
print Person::greet, " ", person1.name, "\n"
puts "another #{Person::greet} #{person1.name}"

require "gem"

string = "base16"
symbol = :base16
fixnum = 0
float  = 0.00
array  = Array.new
array  = ['chris', 85]
hash   = {"test" => "test"}
regexp = /[abc]/

# This is a comment
class Person
  
  attr_accessor :name
  
  def initialize(attributes = {})
    @name = attributes[:name]
  end
  
  def self.greet
    "hello"
  end
end

person1 = Person.new(:name => "Chris")
print Person::greet, " ", person1.name, "\n"
puts "another #{Person::greet} #{person1.name}"

require "gem"

string = "base16"
symbol = :base16
fixnum = 0
float  = 0.00
array  = Array.new
array  = ['chris', 85]
hash   = {"test" => "test"}
regexp = /[abc]/

# This is a comment
class Person
  
  attr_accessor :name
  
  def initialize(attributes = {})
    @name = attributes[:name]
  end
  
  def self.greet
    "hello"
  end
end

person1 = Person.new(:name => "Chris")
print Person::greet, " ", person1.name, "\n"
puts "another #{Person::greet} #{person1.name}"

string = "base16"
symbol = :base16
fixnum = 0
float  = 0.00
array  = Array.new
array  = ['chris', 85]
hash   = {"test" => "test"}

class Person
  
  attr_accessor :name
  
  def initialize(attributes = {})
    @name = attributes[:name]
  end
  
  def self.greet
    "hello"
  end
end

person1 = Person.new(:name => "Chris")
print Person::greet, " ", person1.name, "\n"
puts "another #{Person::greet} #{person1.name}"

require "gem"

string = "base16"
symbol = :base16
fixnum = 0
float  = 0.00
array  = Array.new
array  = ['chris', 85]
hash   = {"test" => "test"}
regexp = /[abc]/

# This is a comment
class Person
  
  attr_accessor :name
  
  def initialize(attributes = {})
    @name = attributes[:name]
  end
  
  def self.greet
    "hello"
  end
end

person1 = Person.new(:name => "Chris")
print Person::greet, " ", person1.name, "\n"
puts "another #{Person::greet} #{person1.name}"

require "gem"

string = "base16"
symbol = :base16
fixnum = 0
float  = 0.00
array  = Array.new
array  = ['chris', 85]
hash   = {"test" => "test"}
regexp = /[abc]/

# This is a comment
class Person
  
  attr_accessor :name
  
  def initialize(attributes = {})
    @name = attributes[:name]
  end
  
  def self.greet
    "hello"
  end
end

person1 = Person.new(:name => "Chris")
print Person::greet, " ", person1.name, "\n"
puts "another #{Person::greet} #{person1.name}"

codeexample-base16-google-light">{% highlight ruby%}
require "gem"

string = "base16"
symbol = :base16
fixnum = 0
float  = 0.00
array  = Array.new
array  = ['chris', 85]
hash   = {"test" => "test"}
regexp = /[abc]/

# This is a comment
class Person
  
  attr_accessor :name
  
  def initialize(attributes = {})
    @name = attributes[:name]
  end
  
  def self.greet
    "hello"
  end
end

person1 = Person.new(:name => "Chris")
print Person::greet, " ", person1.name, "\n"
puts "another #{Person::greet} #{person1.name}"

require "gem"

string = "base16"
symbol = :base16
fixnum = 0
float  = 0.00
array  = Array.new
array  = ['chris', 85]
hash   = {"test" => "test"}
regexp = /[abc]/

# This is a comment
class Person
  
  attr_accessor :name
  
  def initialize(attributes = {})
    @name = attributes[:name]
  end
  
  def self.greet
    "hello"
  end
end

person1 = Person.new(:name => "Chris")
print Person::greet, " ", person1.name, "\n"
puts "another #{Person::greet} #{person1.name}"

require "gem"

string = "base16"
symbol = :base16
fixnum = 0
float  = 0.00
array  = Array.new
array  = ['chris', 85]
hash   = {"test" => "test"}
regexp = /[abc]/

# This is a comment
class Person
  
  attr_accessor :name
  
  def initialize(attributes = {})
    @name = attributes[:name]
  end
  
  def self.greet
    "hello"
  end
end

person1 = Person.new(:name => "Chris")
print Person::greet, " ", person1.name, "\n"
puts "another #{Person::greet} #{person1.name}"

require "gem"

string = "base16"
symbol = :base16
fixnum = 0
float  = 0.00
array  = Array.new
array  = ['chris', 85]
hash   = {"test" => "test"}
regexp = /[abc]/

# This is a comment
class Person
  
  attr_accessor :name
  
  def initialize(attributes = {})
    @name = attributes[:name]
  end
  
  def self.greet
    "hello"
  end
end

person1 = Person.new(:name => "Chris")
print Person::greet, " ", person1.name, "\n"
puts "another #{Person::greet} #{person1.name}"

require "gem"

string = "base16"
symbol = :base16
fixnum = 0
float  = 0.00
array  = Array.new
array  = ['chris', 85]
hash   = {"test" => "test"}
regexp = /[abc]/

# This is a comment
class Person
  
  attr_accessor :name
  
  def initialize(attributes = {})
    @name = attributes[:name]
  end
  
  def self.greet
    "hello"
  end
end

person1 = Person.new(:name => "Chris")
print Person::greet, " ", person1.name, "\n"
puts "another #{Person::greet} #{person1.name}"

require "gem"

string = "base16"
symbol = :base16
fixnum = 0
float  = 0.00
array  = Array.new
array  = ['chris', 85]
hash   = {"test" => "test"}
regexp = /[abc]/

# This is a comment
class Person
  
  attr_accessor :name
  
  def initialize(attributes = {})
    @name = attributes[:name]
  end
  
  def self.greet
    "hello"
  end
end

person1 = Person.new(:name => "Chris")
print Person::greet, " ", person1.name, "\n"
puts "another #{Person::greet} #{person1.name}"

require "gem"

string = "base16"
symbol = :base16
fixnum = 0
float  = 0.00
array  = Array.new
array  = ['chris', 85]
hash   = {"test" => "test"}
regexp = /[abc]/

# This is a comment
class Person
  
  attr_accessor :name
  
  def initialize(attributes = {})
    @name = attributes[:name]
  end
  
  def self.greet
    "hello"
  end
end

person1 = Person.new(:name => "Chris")
print Person::greet, " ", person1.name, "\n"
puts "another #{Person::greet} #{person1.name}"

require "gem"

string = "base16"
symbol = :base16
fixnum = 0
float  = 0.00
array  = Array.new
array  = ['chris', 85]
hash   = {"test" => "test"}
regexp = /[abc]/

# This is a comment
class Person
  
  attr_accessor :name
  
  def initialize(attributes = {})
    @name = attributes[:name]
  end
  
  def self.greet
    "hello"
  end
end

person1 = Person.new(:name => "Chris")
print Person::greet, " ", person1.name, "\n"
puts "another #{Person::greet} #{person1.name}"

require "gem"

string = "base16"
symbol = :base16
fixnum = 0
float  = 0.00
array  = Array.new
array  = ['chris', 85]
hash   = {"test" => "test"}
regexp = /[abc]/

# This is a comment
class Person
  
  attr_accessor :name
  
  def initialize(attributes = {})
    @name = attributes[:name]
  end
  
  def self.greet
    "hello"
  end
end

person1 = Person.new(:name => "Chris")
print Person::greet, " ", person1.name, "\n"
puts "another #{Person::greet} #{person1.name}"
